Local News

Tenth Anniversary of Premier Sun Yat-sen's Death

The Municipal Party Headquarters Held a Memorial Meeting Yesterday, and the Municipal Government Held a Tree Planting Ceremony

Yesterday was the tenth anniversary of the death of Premier Sun Yat-sen. The Municipal Party Headquarters convened representatives from all walks of life at 10 AM in the auditorium of the headquarters to hold a memorial meeting. At the same time, the Municipal Government held a tree-planting ceremony in the city center. Central News Agency reporters specially recorded the events as follows:

Memorial Meeting: The memorial meeting was held at 10 AM in the auditorium of the Municipal Party Headquarters. Representatives from various district party headquarters, district sub-headquarters, representatives from various bureaus of the municipal government, the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Garrison Headquarters, the Municipal Defense Corps, the Ordnance Factory, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, the Municipal Farmers' Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, various trade unions, the First and Second Special District Courts, Dongwu Law School, the National Public School, Zhengfeng College, Patriotic Girls' School, Minli Middle School, Huadong Middle School, and the entire staff of the Labor Movement Training Institute, totaling over seventy organizations, participated, with approximately two hundred attendees. Cai Hongtian presided over the meeting.

Order of the Meeting: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Sing the party anthem; (3) Bow three times to the national flag and the portrait of Premier Sun; (4) The chairman respectfully reads Premier Sun's will; (5) Silent tribute; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Speeches; (8) Slogans; (9) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Cai Hongtian reported, stating that today is the tenth anniversary of the death of Premier Sun Yat-sen in Beijing. While in mourning, we should not only commemorate the great spirit of the Premier but also strive to complete the revolutionary cause. The Premier was the founder of the Party and the state, and the mentor of the revolution. Our commemoration can be divided into three phases: (1) During the Premier's lifetime, the Premier devoted his entire life to the revolutionary cause. From a young age, he aspired to overthrow the Manchu Qing government. As he grew older, he strived with an indomitable spirit to establish the Republic of China and achieve freedom and equality as his responsibility. For forty years, he maintained his fearless spirit, which is truly admirable. (2) The Premier's will includes all revolutionary methods and points out the path to revolution in great detail, such as awakening the masses and uniting with all the nations of the world that treat us as equals to fight together, and instructs us to continue our efforts in accordance with the Three Principles of the People, the National Construction Program, and the Outline of National Construction to thoroughly complete the task. (3) After the Premier's death, the Premier's death was a great loss to our country, and we have still not completed the revolution to this day. However, the entire population and military and political leaders have deeply realized that the Three Principles of the People is the only magic weapon for building China. In addition to vowing allegiance to the Party and the state, there is no other way to consolidate the foundation of the state. Therefore, we are willing to unanimously support the Party and the state, assist the government, because the Three Principles of the People can make the country prosperous, seek common welfare, and provide equality and freedom, and increase production and construction internally, quell external troubles, and abolish unequal treaties. I hope that everyone will work hard and move forward on the right track to comfort his spirit in heaven.

Commemorative Slogans: After the chairman's report, everyone shouted slogans and then announced the adjournment. The slogans are as follows: (1) Inherit Premier Sun's revolutionary spirit; (2) Complete Premier Sun's revolutionary cause; (3) Implement Premier Sun's teachings; (4) Step up production and construction; (5) Complete local autonomy; (6) Strengthen the Party's organization; (7) Premier Sun's spirit is immortal; (8) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; (9) Long live the Republic of China.

Tree Planting Ceremony: Various Party, government, and military organizations in the city held a tree-planting ceremony at 9 AM yesterday in the auditorium of the Municipal Government in the city center. Participants included Mayor Wu, Secretary-General Yu, Director Yang Xiaotian, Director Wu Xingya, Director Cai Zengji, Director Pan Gongzhan, Standing Committee member of the Municipal Party Headquarters Tong Xingbai, Zhou Xianzhang of the Naval Headquarters, Cai Ren of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, Lu Youchang of the Jianghai Customs Supervision Office, Yu Zhenhui of the Municipal Farmers' Association, section chiefs, secretaries, and staff members of various bureaus and offices under the Municipal Government, teachers and students from various schools, and representatives from various organizations, totaling over a thousand people. After the music played and the meeting was opened and the ceremony was performed, Mayor Wu gave a report, followed by speeches by Tong Xingbai, a standing committee member of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Wu Xingya, director of the Social Affairs Bureau. Mayor Wu then led the participants to take a photo in front of the steps, and then to the third branch of the Municipal Garden on Fudongqian Road to plant trees.

Mayor's Report: Mayor Wu said in his report that today is the day to commemorate the death of Premier Sun Yat-sen, and it is also Arbor Day. We hold these ceremonies every year. The Premier's great personality and fearless spirit created a great revolutionary cause for the country and the nation. This is our everlasting model. When we commemorate such a great figure, we should of course have a very concrete and practical movement to express our sincere commemorative psychology. The so-called Arbor Day is to promote a movement of afforestation. Afforestation is a basic construction of the national economy, because forests are closely related to our national economy and people's livelihood. Our needs in life, food, clothing, shelter, and transportation, are all directly related to forests. If we want to revitalize the Chinese countryside, to have a foundation for China's economic construction, and to ensure that the supply of necessities for the Chinese people is not difficult, then we cannot ignore this afforestation movement. Therefore, we also hold a tree-planting ceremony on the day of commemorating the death of Premier Sun, so that the Premier's greatness can be continued, endlessly, and not be ignored by our nation. This is the tenth anniversary of Premier Sun's death, and in each year's commemoration, we feel that its meaning is different. The Premier's great personality and great cause are not only a model for our Chinese nation for all generations, but also his life of hardship, struggling for the country and the nation, and fighting against the autocratic monarchs and warlord politicians of the Manchu Qing Dynasty, lasted for decades. Although there were more than ten failures, he continued to work hard until the last moment of his death, shouting the遗言 of "peace," "struggle," and "save China." This is a spirit that we, who are responsible for building the country, cannot forget for a moment, and we will surely succeed. In the past ten years, can our surviving comrades and compatriots across the country inherit his spirit, complete his cause, and realize his principles, after Premier Sun's forty years of struggle? This is something we should reflect on. Looking around at the current environment, the crisis of the country and the nation's destiny cannot but make us alarmed, so we should make such a resolution to do ten days' work in one day, one month's work in ten days, one year's work in one month, and ten years' work in one year. We, with a spirit of hard work and straightforwardness, will catch up head-on, and in this way, we can achieve success in our personal careers, as well as in the careers of the country and society. We must recognize that the Premier's great personality, fearless spirit, and spirit of fighting for the nation and the country are the work of saving the country and preserving its existence.

Speeches by Tong and Wu: Tong Xingbai then gave a speech, stating that today is the tenth anniversary of Premier Sun's death, and we are also holding a tree-planting ceremony. Mayor Wu has already reported in detail on the significance of tree planting, and I will not say more. I would like to take this opportunity to talk about the relationship between the Premier Sun Memorial and tree planting. Why do we have these two actions on the day of the Premier Sun Memorial? Regarding our proclaiming the Premier's doctrine and his cause on this day, and encouraging us to inherit his spirit and complete his cause, this is a commemoration in terms of the spiritual aspect. In addition, we hold a tree-planting ceremony on this day, and we hold it every year. After twenty or thirty years, or even two or three hundred years, it can be said that the country's forests are all in memory of the Premier's death. This is a memorial expression in terms of the material aspect. We can have two feelings here. First, trees have the virtue of "timely revival." The growth, development, and prosperity of trees is a manifestation of nature, and we humans must also have this virtue of "timely revival." China has now reached a time of great danger, and international relations are also very dangerous. The suffering of people's livelihood in the country is also extremely urgent. Now the trees are reviving in time, and we should all work hard and be excited in time to save the nation and the country. Second, there are no useless trees. No matter how big or small, thick or thin, each has its use. This also shows us that we are a member of the nation, and we should all fulfill our responsibilities to the country and society and become a useful person. If there are people among us who cannot be self-reliant, then they are not as good as trees. Therefore, on this commemorative day, we should earnestly review ourselves and contribute all our abilities to the country and the nation. Finally, Wu Xingya, Director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, gave a speech, stating that today we are commemorating the death of Premier Sun, and we cannot help but recall that when the Premier was dying, he was still issuing the calls for "peace," "struggle," and "save China." We feel that peace and struggle are based on the spirit of China's inherent kingly way, and saving China is also saving the world, because China's position is not only a center of gravity in East Asia, but also bears a great mission in the world. If China cannot be rich and strong, it will extend from the Far East to the world, and all will return to the Great Harmony. Therefore, we must not forget these seven words for a moment.

Tree Planting Situation: After the ceremony, Mayor Wu led the participants to walk to Fudongqian Road. Amidst the melodious sounds of military music, they entered the third branch of the Municipal Garden. First, Mayor Wu personally shoveled the soil and planted trees, followed by Secretary-General Yu, Director Yang, Director Wu, Committee Member Dong, and Director Pan. The trees planted by Mayor Wu were located in the center of the first row at the entrance. Secretary-General Yu, Director Yang, and Councilor Luo followed behind him, and the trees were arranged in a row. The other directors and the Jianghai Customs and other bureaus of the Municipal Party Headquarters were arranged on both sides. Various schools were located on both sides of the grassland in the back. The site was planted at 1:30 PM and then the meeting was adjourned.

Tree Planting on Two Railways: The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration and the special party department of the two railways jointly held a memorial ceremony for the tenth anniversary of Premier Sun's death and a tree-planting ceremony at the Qingyanggang Railway Garden Hotel yesterday. Wu Shaozeng, the acting director of the railway administration, Chen Chengshi, Li Dasan, Song Chuanji, representatives of the special party department, and more than 100 section chiefs, deputy section chiefs, and comrades from the two railway party departments attended. At 8 AM, they took a special train prepared by the railway administration from Shanghai North Station, attached to the fourth Shanghai-Beijing express train. At 9:30 AM, they held a ceremony in the hotel, presented wreaths, and read a eulogy. Wu Shaozeng, the acting director, delivered a speech on behalf of the railway administration, stating that the Premier's life embodied the three immortal qualities of establishing virtue, establishing meritorious service, and establishing words. The Three Principles of the People and the Five-Power Constitution written by the Premier were profound and extensive, and were admired by both China and foreign countries. This was establishing words; hand-founding the Republic of China was establishing meritorious service; the establishment of virtue was so great that it cannot be described in words. The most important thing is the two points of universal love and integrity. The Premier sacrificed everything to save the country and the people, which is the manifestation of his spirit of universal love. When the Premier died, the only thing left in his home was books, which is the manifestation of his spirit of integrity. We commemorate the Premier by continuing the Premier's aspirations and learning from the Premier's character. Universal love and integrity are the basic conditions for being a person, and we must practice them personally and implement them practically. Integrity is a passive effort; as long as you restrain yourself, it is not difficult to achieve. Universal love is an active behavior; not only must you have the thought, but also the methods. For example, when we see passengers crowding, or someone encounters a disaster, we feel unbearable, and at the same time, we try our best to eliminate their crowding and eliminate their disaster. This is one aspect of universal love. The above two points are the most important, and I hope to encourage everyone to work together on them. At the end, he explained the significance of tree planting, and said that the designated planting this time is on both banks of Qingyanggang. Today opens the beginning, and in the future, it will be jointly promoted with the local authorities, in order to gradually popularize the river banks, and one day the green trees will provide a benefit to travelers. After the speech, they took a photo together, and then went to plant trees along the river. The trees were planted with peach and willow trees, planted in intervals, winding for over a mile. They did not return to Shanghai until 12:50 PM.

Business as Usual: Yesterday, all agencies, schools, factories, shops, and legal entities, in addition to sending representatives to participate in the memorial meeting for the death of Premier Sun Yat-sen convened by the Municipal Party Headquarters and the tree-planting ceremony of the Municipal Government, all continued to work as usual and did not take a holiday. The schools each convened meetings to report on the significance of the commemoration of Premier Sun's death and tree planting. The various organizations and schools lowered their flags to half-mast to express their condolences. Military and police agencies, such as the Emergency Defense Department, and the French Concession Police Department took a holiday to commemorate the day, as stipulated by the consul. Therefore, the criminal public prosecution case of the Second Special District Court was suspended yesterday due to the suspension of the Police Department. At 9 AM, Liang and Wang, the two presidents of the Senior Court and the Second Special Court, Zhao and Chen, the two chief inspectors, and other officials and staff led the inspection and held a memorial ceremony in the first courtroom auditorium. After completion, civil and criminal self-prosecution, civil and criminal appeals cases were still tried as usual.

Japanese Commemoration: The Shanghai Office of the Japanese Embassy and the Japanese Consulate General in Shanghai took a day off to commemorate the Premier.

Kong Xiangxi and Others Go to Beijing

Kong Xiangxi, Xu Tingyao, Yang Dezhao, Chen Diaoyuan, and Jing Tingyi took the night train to Beijing yesterday.

Envoy to Cuba, Ling Bing, Returns to China Yesterday

Will Return to His Ancestral Home in Gushi, Henan

Our country's envoy to Cuba, Mr. Ling Bing, returned to China on the 23rd of last month aboard the Japanese Empress. Yesterday afternoon, he arrived in Shanghai by the same ship, accompanied by his wife, son, and General Zhang Fakui. Mr. Ling told a Central News Agency reporter on board that he had been abroad for five years and had specifically requested leave to return home to visit family and attend to personal matters. Having left Cuba over a month ago, he was somewhat out of touch with the latest situation. The Cuban government has very good relations with our overseas Chinese, with no instances of oppression or expulsion. The Cuban people are the same, to the point of not distinguishing nationalities. However, the instability of their political situation has had some impact on various undertakings. There are approximately 20,000 to 30,000 overseas Chinese in Cuba. Recently, due to the global economic crisis, Cuba has inevitably been affected, causing larger-scale Chinese business operators to go bankrupt. Some, due to difficult living conditions, were forced to return to China, while others are waiting for opportunities to continue. Small-scale operators are still managing to barely maintain themselves. After reporting to Beijing, I will return to my ancestral home in Gushi, Henan, for a short stay to rest, he said.

Sino-Russian Daosheng Bank Liquidation Office Opposes the Eastern Railway Deal

Shiye She reports that the illegal sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway has attracted considerable attention from various countries. In addition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs instructing our ambassador to Russia, Yan, to lodge a strong protest, the General Liquidation Office of the Sino-Russian Daosheng Bank in this city has also expressed its firm opposition and will make a corresponding statement when the formal signing takes place. Yesterday was the date for Japan and Russia to hold the initialing ceremony. A Shiye She reporter specifically visited Mr. Yaldensky, the Russian advisor to the Daosheng Bank, to inquire about his views. According to him, this office, in any case, fundamentally cannot and will not recognize this illegal transaction between Japan and Russia. Therefore, this office had already sent formal statements to the Japanese Minister, Arimasa Akira, the Soviet Russian Ambassador to China, Bogomolov, and the government authorities of both parties last month, requesting the preservation of all rights and interests related to the railway and refusing to accept any restrictions. Numerous letters were sent to both sides, but no response has been received. Currently, I am paying close attention to the cause and effect and the extent of the development of this transaction. It is not convenient to disclose at this time what forms of opposition will be taken. In summary, this office will definitely respond with effective measures. This office not only expresses sympathy for the Chinese government's opposition but is also willing to do its utmost to lead the way. Mr. Ya added that it may be possible to meet and discuss with the Russian ambassador, Mr. Bogomolov, when he comes to China at the end of the month.

Zhang Fakui Returned to China Yesterday, Arriving in Shanghai: Talks About How European and American Countries are All Striving to Become Stronger; Future Plans Not Yet Fully Decided

General Zhang Fakui, having traveled around Europe and America and investigated various aspects of politics, economics, military affairs, and society in various countries for nearly three years, recently, having almost completed his travels in European and American countries, returned to China on the Japanese Empress from Canada on the 23rd of last month. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday and is staying at the New Asia Hotel. A Central News Agency reporter specially investigated the situation, as follows:

Arrived in Shanghai in the Afternoon

The Japanese Empress arrived at the Qichang Wharf at 5:30 PM yesterday. In advance, more than ten of Mr. Zhang's relatives and friends boarded the Jianghai Customs' small tugboat Jinghui to meet him at the Wusongkou. They also toured Donggou in Pudong while waiting. Only when the Japanese Empress approached did they join the ship. Mr. and Mrs. Zhang waved and tipped their hats to the welcomers on the ship, with great joy.

Welcoming Personnel

The municipal government sent the Yue Shi ship, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent a public security ship carrying the welcoming personnel. Those who boarded the ship to welcome him included Tang Shixuan, representing Mayor Wu, Yang Dezhao, representing Chen Jitang, Yang Hu, the director of the Municipal Security Department, Huang Jianping, representing Li Zongren, Yu Ming, the director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, He Zhuoxian, the director of the Trademark Bureau, and Mr. Zhang's relatives and friends, totaling over a hundred people. The Water Police Bureau also dispatched police to provide strict protection.

Future Plans

Mr. Zhang was wearing a dark brown suit, a black woolen overcoat, and a dark gray hat. He appeared stronger and slightly more prosperous than when he left the country, with a radiant appearance. When the Japanese Empress docked, the welcoming personnel crowded onto the ship. Mr. Zhang greeted them warmly, full of energy. Accompanying him were Mr. Zhang's wife and Mr. and Mrs. Ling Bing, the envoy to Cuba. According to Mr. Zhang, speaking to a Central News Agency reporter, after arriving in Shanghai, he will stay at the New Asia Hotel to rest. His future plans have not yet been decided.

Written Statement

Mr. Zhang issued a written statement, outlining his journey, stating, "Since I resigned from my military position in October of the 21st year of the Republic [1932] and received government funding to travel abroad, nearly three years have passed in an instant. During this period, I traveled to over twenty countries in Europe and America, and what I have seen and heard is difficult to summarize in a single sentence. However, in general, although the political systems of various countries have differences, the sizes of their territories vary, and the strength of their national power differs, since the European War, all countries, aware of the tragedy of national subjugation, have shown a spirit of striving and possess a new atmosphere. Their patriotism and belief in national self-determination are particularly vigorous in all countries. The hard work of Turkey, the arduous struggle of Germany, the diligent governance of Italy, and the perfection of the naval, land, and air equipment of the strong countries of England, France, the United States, and Italy are all admirable. Observing the various backward conditions in our country, one cannot help but feel a chill. Therefore, I believe that if our country today wants to survive in this threatening and turbulent environment, the only way is to be united from top to bottom, to thoroughly awaken, to abandon selfish and self-serving ideas, to prioritize the country and the nation, and to work hard, so that in the future, national disasters may be slightly averted."

Government and Banking Industries Prepare Credit Loans to Revive the Market

A Total of 5 Million Yuan, Equally Assigned, Separate Meetings of Banking and Money Industries Associations

Xinsheng She reports that the Local Association, in order to revive the market, has, through a special committee's research, proposed that the government and the banking and money industries each contribute 2.5 million yuan, totaling 5 million yuan, to provide credit loans for industry and commerce. A syndicate will be organized to manage the loans. After approval by the relevant groups, a request will be submitted to Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi for adoption. In the future, after implementation, the interest rates on loan applications will be specially reduced, with the sole purpose of reviving the market in the hope of recovery.

Separate Meetings of Banking and Money Industries

After the banking and money industries associations received a letter from the Local Association requesting the provision of credit loans for industry and commerce, the money industry association held an executive committee meeting the night before last to discuss the matter. Due to the importance of the matter, it was decided to submit it to the general meeting of member representatives for a public vote. The association will convene the meeting within a few days. The banking industry association is scheduled to hold an executive committee meeting tomorrow afternoon to discuss the matter.

To Be Submitted to the Ministry for Adoption After a Decision

It is heard that after the banking and money industries associations meet, the City Chamber of Commerce, the Local Association, and the banking and money industries associations will hold a joint meeting to study the specific implementation measures. After a solution is found, it will be submitted to the Minister of Finance. During the meeting, the topic of these issues was discussed.

Various Industries Hope for Early Implementation

A Xinsheng She reporter learned from various important industries yesterday morning that after the market revival plan is decided, the Local Association will have the government and the banking and money industries each contribute 5 million yuan for credit loans, according to the plan. After approval by the relevant groups, a request will be submitted to Minister Kong for implementation. Currently, industry and commerce are in severe decline and are difficult to maintain. Therefore, everyone hopes that these credit loans can be implemented as soon as possible to alleviate business difficulties. As for the loan scheme with goods as collateral, it is also hoped that the government and the banking and money industries will adopt and implement it as much as possible, it was said.

Measures Pending Decision by the Syndicate

For the credit loans, the banking and money industries will each contribute 2.5 million yuan, which will be divided equally by the member banks of the banking association and the member money shops of the money industry association, each contributing 1.25 million yuan. Any shop or factory in the Shanghai area that is owned by Chinese capital may apply for a loan, using a joint guarantee method. However, it is still necessary to wait for the establishment of the syndicate before further discussions and decisions are made.

Increase in Chinese Goods Exported to the US in January This Year

The Great American Evening Post reports that according to statistics released today (the 12th) by the US Consul General's Office in Shanghai, China's exports to the United States in January this year were worth a total of US$5,928,194, a significant increase compared to December and November of last year. The total value in December last year was $4,341,630, and in November it was only $3,036,872. Among the exports in January, inedible plant products ranked first, with a total value of $2,045,175. Second were inedible animal products and animal products, with a total value of $1,344,678. Third were textiles, with a total value of $1,080,666.

The Opening Date of the Art Exhibition Preview is Not Yet Set

Exhibits Can Be Put on Display Starting on the 20th

A Central News Agency report states that the London Exhibition of Chinese Art preview has been actively selecting antiques and arranging the venue for the past month. However, because the selection work is time-consuming, the opening date will be at the earliest at the end of the month. The rumor that it will open on the 20th is not accurate. A Central News Agency reporter visited the person in charge of the exhibition yesterday to inquire about the latest situation, and received the following replies:

British Commissioners Have Arrived in Shanghai

A total of five commissioners specially appointed by the London Exhibition of Chinese Art to come to China to select antiques for exhibition in England have arrived. Among them, Sir David, Raphael Hobson, and Ormofu Polus have arrived in Shanghai and are staying at the Cathay Hotel. The day before yesterday, Yang Zhensheng of the exhibition specially hosted a banquet for the four commissioners at Wen Yuanning's residence, accompanied by Ma Heng, Wen Yuanning, and Zhao Tiezhang, to strengthen their relationships.

Visited Antiques Yesterday Morning

Yesterday morning, the four British commissioners came to the exhibition to view ancient paintings, hosted by Yang Zhensheng, Ma Heng, Gu Shusen, and Wen Yuanning. They praised the ancient art of our country very sincerely but did not express any special opinions. They will leave Shanghai after the preview closes, while David and Raphael will take a detour through Japan and America to select ancient Chinese art owned by American collectors for collection and transport to England for exhibition.

Antiques from Various Places Have Been Delivered

The antiques from various places participating in the preview have generally been delivered. However, ancient woodblock prints and other items collected by the Peking Library and various antiques obtained from archaeological excavations by the Academia Sinica have not yet arrived in Shanghai. The exhibition has already sent a telegram urging them, and they should also be delivered soon.

Review Work Will Be Completed

Regarding the review of antiques, bronzes have been completed, and calligraphy and painting have also been largely completed. In terms of porcelain, Ming porcelain will be reviewed today. Today, the calligraphy and painting on fans will also be inspected on Tianzhutang Street.

External Affairs Department Reassigns Assistant

In addition, Wu Zexiang, specially assigned by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to assist the exhibition with foreign affairs, has now been transferred to Sichuan by order of the Ministry and replaced by Zhao Tiezhang, the section chief of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

Additional Glass Cabinets

The renovation of the venue has been completed. However, 64 glass cabinets for displaying antiques were originally ordered from the Dahua Iron Factory and have all been delivered to the exhibition, but they are still not enough. Thirty more were added and will all be delivered before the 20th. Therefore, starting from the 20th, exhibits can be put on display.

Requesting Half of the Fee to Be Allocated for Disaster Relief

Guowen She reports that the Land Disaster Relief Association in the Renji Charity Hall on Yunnan Road in this city has received representatives from various disaster areas who have continued to come and request funds, but the relief funds have already been allocated and there is nothing to do. It happened that the antiques being transported to England were exhibited in Shanghai in advance and a small viewing fee was collected. The association recently requested the antique preview to allocate half of the viewing fee to the association to prepare for disaster relief. It is now learned that the preview exhibition is considering the matter is of great importance and will submit it to the Nanjing Antiquities Preservation Committee for instructions.

The City Chamber of Commerce Again Sends a Letter to the Public Works Department to Stop Telephone Price Increases

Whether from a Public Welfare or a Commercial Perspective, Public Interests Should Not Be Extorted Again

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the Public Works Department of the International Settlement, stating, "To the honorable department, on January 30th of this year, this chamber, according to letters from the silk and satin industry, the dyeing and weaving industry, and 26 other industry associations, stated that the Shanghai Telephone Company, at a time when the city's commerce is collapsing, is discussing increasing telephone fees for citizens, which disregards public welfare and only seeks private gain. We request that you negotiate to cancel it, etc. We immediately sent letter No. 1567 of the Pu character, requesting your department to consider the public interest and stop it, which is on record. More than a month has passed, and we have not yet received a reply. Now, we have received another letter from the book industry association, which states, 'Newspapers are reporting that telephone prices in this port are about to increase. Telephones are a means of transportation, and commercial markets have regarded them as necessities, like grains and water, as a type of expense. In recent years, due to the global economic downturn, industries in this port have been in recession and suffering deeply. The telephone company suddenly has an increase in prices, wanting to increase profits alone, which is unreasonable. We request that you forward this to the Public Works Department for practical prevention, etc.' According to the Public Utilities Report column in the sixth issue, ninth volume, of your department's gazette, the company's request to amend the price list is to increase its total revenue by 22.89% and increase the annual interest on its invested capital to about 10%, of which 2% is for the general reserve fund. This chamber believes that if the company requested a price increase based on the previous contract with your department when the market was stable, it would still be reasonable. Now, the market is so depressed, and the number of shops, factories, and industries that are in a state of semi-suspension is unprecedented. According to its own report, the Shanghai Telephone Company was still able to obtain a net profit of 6.13% in 1934, which is a rare profit in commerce. Whether from a public welfare perspective or purely from a commercial perspective, public interests should not be extorted again to increase its income. We correspondently request your department, for the sake of the interests of the majority of citizens, to not approve the case, which is our utmost hope."

Zhou Anren, Yang Baohe, Chen Jinkui, Zhang Qingqi, Lu Yishun, and Li Hongfa, overseas Chinese residing in Chiba Prefecture and Gunma Prefecture, Japan, and Zhuo Zi (Japanese nationality), the wife of Lin Zhenqing, and son, from the previous twenty-sixth group of expelled refugees, totaling nine people, arrived in Shanghai yesterday on the Dollar Steamship Company's President Hoover. Japanese Newspaper Claims Japanese Goods Imports are Not Strong

Claims it is Due to the Poor State of Chinese Society

The Japanese-language Mainichi Shimbun reports that since the development of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, rumors have spread that imports of Japanese goods have gradually increased. However, although the voice of anti-Japanese sentiment has subsided, the financial pressure and exchange rate fluctuations in China, judging from the state of transactions in various aspects, have not made any progress. Recently, the Shanghai branch of the Nippon Yusen Kaisha, regarding the Mikasa Maru, which was imported today (the 13th), said that although there were 2,500 tons of goods, excluding 800 tons of rice and cotton, it was still not a full ship. In addition, the Asama Maru had 1,600 tons of cargo, but it did not reach six-tenths of the full ship. This is enough to prove that the import of Japanese goods has not increased in any way, but has only maintained the status quo. In the past, due to anti-Japanese relations, Japanese goods could not be imported, but now there is no anti-Japanese movement, and the reason why imports are not strong is due to the poor state of society in general.

The National Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs the Ministry of Finance to Delay the Implementation of the New Regulations on Wine Tax in Chahar Province

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, stating, "We have investigated that our association previously received a letter from the representatives of the chambers of commerce of various counties in Chahar Province, stating that the new regulations on wine tax in Chahar Province are harsh, and the people cannot bear it. We request that you forward this to the council for reduction. Our association has telegraphed the council twice to request this, which is on record. Recently, the representatives of the chambers of commerce of the province, Wang Youzhi, Cui Yunshan, Wei Tai, and Li Kuan, came to the council to state everything and said that they had already petitioned your ministry and the Tax Affairs Administration. In view of this, we have further investigated that the Chahar Province Tobacco and Wine Tax Bureau has changed from contract amount to actual collection this time. In principle, the wine merchants in Chahar Province do not oppose it. However, the tax rate is several times higher than that of neighboring Hebei Province, which is difficult to maintain business. Some have been forced to voluntarily close their businesses, and the Chahar Province Tobacco and Wine Tax Bureau must forcibly pay half a year of closure fees, otherwise they will be sealed and detained. The harsh situation is unbearable. Chahar Province is adjacent to the border, and strong neighbors are eyeing it. At a time when foreign troubles are deepening, extra care should be given to the situation. If we act rashly, there is a danger of harming fish and inciting birds. It is reasonable to telegraph your ministry again for review and approval. We sincerely request that you quickly order the release of the seals and people, delay the implementation of the new regulations, cancel the closure fees, revise the tax rate according to Hebei, and temporarily collect taxes according to the old regulations until the new regulations are formulated, in order to relieve the people's livelihood and alleviate the difficulties of merchants. Sincerely, the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China."

Western Constable Beats a Vegetable Vendor to Death. A Petition is Filed with the Court Requesting Summons of Witnesses for Investigation. Representatives of the Municipal Federation Branch Call for Investigation of the Facts in Preparation for Negotiations.

According to the New Voice News Agency, after a Western constable from the Putuo Road Police Station No. 62 beat a vegetable vendor to death, the Fourth District Branch of the Municipal Federation of Citizens held a meeting the previous day and appointed Chen Weiwen, Liang Ruiting, Zhu Qizhen, Wu Shuying, and Wang Xianggu as five representatives to petition the Municipal Federation to assist the victim, Zhao Yongru, in negotiating for punishment of the murderer and compensation, and to retain Wang Xianggu and Wu Shaoshan as lawyers to represent Zhao Yongru and draft a petition requesting the Procuratorate of the First Special District Court to summon witnesses for investigation. The original petition stated: "A Western constable from the Putuo Road Police Station No. 62 chased and beat a female civilian, causing her to fall to the ground and die. We respectfully request that you promptly summon witnesses for investigation so that we can negotiate with the Public Works Bureau for the punishment of the murderer and compensation. Zhao Yongru lives at No. 76 Zhujiawan, Zhabei, and has been making a living by farming. She has a daughter named Liujiali, who is eighteen years old this year. On the morning of the 5th of this month, at around 7 a.m., she and her grandmother, Zhao Zhangshi, carried vegetables to the side of the road in the Lide Oil Factory Lane on Yichang Road in western Shanghai to sell them. Suddenly, a Western constable from the Putuo Road Police Station No. 62 came over and interfered without asking the reason, first hitting her grandmother on the head with a baton. The female civilian, seeing this, immediately fled into the lane. However, the Western constable chased after her relentlessly, caught up, and struck her on the back of the head with his hand, causing her to fall to the ground immediately. Her grandmother rushed forward to help her up, but the Western constable kicked her in the waist and did not allow her to help. At that time, many onlookers gathered around and wanted to come forward to help, but they were all kicked or slapped and driven away, not allowed to rescue her. By the time the police car sent her to the hospital, it was too late to save her, and she died shortly thereafter. In addition to her grandmother, Zhao Zhangshi, and vegetable vendors Hou Zhangshi and Xu Zhangshi, who have testified that the chase and beating were true, there are also eyewitnesses who bought vegetables: Wang Tianjin, Gu Chuanshi, and Ji Xiaomei (addresses listed below), who are all important witnesses and can also be summoned for questioning. Under the broad daylight, the residents of the area all know the situation, and it would not be difficult to send personnel to investigate. In short, the facts of this case are clear and the evidence is conclusive, and the Western constable cannot deny it with empty words. Yongru is over half a century old and has only this one daughter. All the vegetables she grows depend on her and her grandmother going to the streets to sell them to earn a living. Unexpectedly, the Western constable used his foreign power and acted lawlessly, beating her to death, not only cutting off Yongru's only remaining lifeline but also putting Yongru's entire family in a dead end. As long as there is breath, we vow to avenge this grievance. Moreover, the Western constable not only does not bow his head and submit to the law but dares to confuse black and white and collude with witnesses to deny the facts. If this is not thoroughly investigated, the truth will be difficult to reveal. If the Western constable is allowed to go scot-free, then the lives of citizens will be in danger. Although the Western constable is British and our country's courts are subject to consular jurisdiction and cannot accept the case, for the sake of initiating negotiations, it is extremely convenient for your court to investigate the facts and collect evidence. We believe that the great British Empire has always been known for its spirit of the rule of law and will not destroy it because of the Western constable. This matter concerns the dignity of the nation and the lives of the people. Therefore, we specially submit this petition and cry out to your court to examine and approve it, promptly summon witnesses for investigation, so that we can negotiate with the Public Works Bureau for the punishment of the murderer and compensation, in order to maintain the dignity of the nation and avenge this grievance. Furthermore, we previously received notice of the results of the autopsy, and we ask for instructions so that we can study them. Mother Ren Dewei respectfully submits this petition to the Procuratorate of the First Special District Local Court."

The International Trade Bureau Introduces Domestic Products

American Merchants Need Chinese Cinnamon. Swedish Merchants are Willing to Sell Our Textiles.

American Demand for Cinnamon

According to the International Trade Bureau at the New Rubbish Bridge yesterday, cinnamon is produced in the provinces of Guangdong and Guangxi and Guizhou, accounting for about 65% of the world's production. The cultivation of cinnamon trees is particularly prevalent in the counties south of the West River in Guangxi Province, between Xunzhou and Pingnan Yulin. Every year, it is transported to foreign countries via Guangzhou, mainly to the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, India, and other countries. It is used to make spices and medicines, as it has properties that stimulate, strengthen, replenish, dispel wind, and astringe. Therefore, in medicine, it can treat internal wind, abdominal pain, diarrhea, and other symptoms. After cinnamon is distilled into oil, it is also an indispensable raw material for making perfume and scented soap. Recently, the New York Chinese Chamber of Commerce sent a letter stating that an importer in the United States needs Chinese cinnamon. We hope that exporters will send a letter to the guidance department of the bureau for introduction.

Swedish Sale of Textiles

In addition, the Swedish Weisheng Company sent a letter stating that it is willing to manage and sell Chinese printed rayon fabrics and cotton fabrics. Manufacturers who wish to seek sales abroad can send a letter to the bureau to request introduction.

Provisional Tax Collection Measures for Plant Cake Made into Feed

The Jianghai Customs Notified Everyone Yesterday

Tang Hai'an, the superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Luo Fude, the customs commissioner, issued a joint notice No. 1435 yesterday regarding the provisional tax collection measures for feed made from plant cake, such as vegetable seed cake, which stated: "We have now received an order from the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance stating that all plant feed made from a mixture of corn seed cake, sorghum seed cake, bean seed cake, peanut cake, and wheat bran, which are not specified in the current export tariff, should be temporarily classified under item 142 (feed) of the export tariff and be subject to an export tax of 5% ad valorem, starting from March 6th of this year. You should comply with this order, etc. We should comply with this order and notify all merchants. We hereby issue this notice."

Copyright Lawsuit over the New History of Yuan

The Book and Newspaper Cooperative Society is Accused of Unauthorized Reprinting. Ke Changsi and His Brothers File a Lawsuit.

Ke Shaomin, a Hanlin scholar of the late Qing Dynasty, lived in seclusion in the former capital after the fall of the Qing Dynasty, living as a reclusive old gentleman, using writing to entertain himself. After his death, his remaining works were all held by his sons Ke Changsi, Changji, Changfen, and Yongxi. Among them, the most valuable and worthy of passing down to future generations is the book "New History of Yuan," which consists of 256 volumes. Initially, it was not published. Later, Changsi and others submitted a request to the Ministry of Interior of the National Government to register and obtain the copyright, and then submitted the original manuscript to the Kaiming Bookstore in the city for publication. The advance subscription for the Twenty-Five Histories issued by the bookstore last summer was to combine the original Twenty-Four Histories with the New History of Yuan into one book. However, shortly thereafter, the Book and Newspaper Cooperative Society also advertised the advance subscription for the Twenty-Six Histories, with a price lower than Kaiming's. The publication date was within January of this year. At that time, Kaiming had negotiated with the society, and now the Ke brothers, after learning that the New History of Yuan was also included in the Twenty-Six Histories, and that it was purely a reprint of their late father's original work, which violated Article 33 of the Publication Law, hired lawyer Sun Zuji to file a criminal lawsuit against Tan Tian, the person in charge of the Book and Newspaper Cooperative Society, requesting that he be punished according to law. They also stated that they reserved all losses suffered by the defendant due to the infringement of copyright, and would file another lawsuit after determining the exact amount of the losses. Yesterday afternoon, Ye Shengchao, the judge of the First Special District Local Court, summoned the defendant. The defendant also hired a lawyer to file a counterclaim against the plaintiffs. According to lawyer Sun, the plaintiffs are all in Beiping, and the defendant's counterclaim is a means of delaying the lawsuit. The court stated that since the defendant had filed a counterclaim, it was necessary for the plaintiffs to appear in court in person, and ordered the hearing to be rescheduled for the afternoon of the 26th of this month.

Gynecologists Cai Songchun and Others are Accused

A Pregnant Woman Miscarries After Taking Medicine. They are Prosecuted for Negligent Injury.

Cai Songchun and Cai Bochun, grandsons of Cai Xiaoxiang, a famous gynecologist in Jiangwan, inherited their grandfather's mantle and practiced medicine at No. 5, Lane 1, Jishanli, East and West Huade Roads. Business was not bad. Recently, Ms. Chen Jiang, a native of Ningbo, the wife of Chen Yuying (an employee of the Ning-Shao Life Insurance Company) residing at No. 173 Gongping Road, hired lawyer Shen Zengkuan to file a lawsuit with the First Special Court, accusing Cai and others of negligent injury. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiang Yinghua presided over the hearing in the Second Criminal Court. The defendants also hired lawyers Lu Qi and Chen Guocai to defend them. The plaintiff, Chen Jiang, stated that she was 32 years old, a native of Ningbo. She had given birth six times since marrying Chen Ziying. Her health had been good since her last birth in June of last year. In October, her menstrual cycle came. Recently, she suddenly felt unwell, and her menstruation had not come for three months. She was suspicious and feared that she was pregnant again. Unable to decide for herself, she went to the defendants' clinic for treatment on February 10 of this year. She explained her situation and asked whether she was unwell or pregnant. After taking her pulse, the defendants concluded that she had a menstrual disorder and was not pregnant. Treatment should be given quickly. They prescribed a prescription, and she purchased the medicine and decocted it. After four treatments, around February 20, she suddenly saw blood. But her discomfort worsened. She went back for treatment and took the medicine. On the 23rd, she had unbearable abdominal pain. After 7 p.m., she suddenly miscarried. Only then did she realize that the defendants had made a wrong diagnosis and had been negligent in their duties. Therefore, she filed a lawsuit and submitted the prescription. Her husband, Chen Ziying, also submitted a statement. When questioned, the defendants stated that when the plaintiff came to see them on February 10, they determined that she was pregnant after taking her pulse. Therefore, the medicines prescribed were all products that nourish the blood and regulate qi. Although the word "pregnancy" was not written on the prescription, this was because there were various inconveniences for gynecologists, so it was not stated explicitly. After several treatments, the plaintiff had recovered by the 14th. On the 22nd, the plaintiff came again, saying that she had accidentally lifted heavy objects, causing her to see blood again. This was due to her own carelessness, and they carefully diagnosed and treated her and tried to calm the fetus. Therefore, it would not have led to an abortion by taking the medicine they had prescribed. The defendants' lawyers argued that the prescription should be sent to the National Medical Association for identification. The judge announced that the case would be heard again in seven days.

Venus: A Dancer Dies Tragically from an Abortion

Dancing While Heavily Pregnant, an Abortion Leads to Death

Bao Huiying, a dancer from Xuzhou at the Weiner Qi (also known as La Dahua) dance hall on North Sichuan Road, is twenty-three years old. She lives with her father, Bao Zhenyuan, at 13 Sanxing Lane, North Sichuan Road. Bao has no formal husband. Recently, she suddenly became pregnant. By the end of last month, she was three months pregnant. Bao's profession involves being embraced by patrons. Once pregnant, her abdomen would swell, inevitably hindering her business. Moreover, as an unmarried woman, being pregnant would significantly damage her reputation. Therefore, she consulted with acquaintances about a suitable solution. The result was that abortion was the only option. On the 4th of this month, she went to Liu Wang, a seventy-three-year-old midwife at 723 Jiujiang Road, requesting an abortion. The agreed-upon price was twenty-four yuan. Ms. Liu applied a plaster to Bao's navel and gave her some pills to take. However, after a night, there was no effect. The next day, she went again, and Ms. Liu changed the plaster, applying it to her navel, and performed a procedure, massaging Bao's abdomen for a while before instructing her to return home. That evening, a piece of flesh in Bao's abdomen did indeed come out, which seemed promising. However, a day or two later, Bao had a slight diarrhea. She inquired with Ms. Liu, who told her that she only needed to consume a little hot porridge to recover. Bao followed her instructions, and initially, it seemed to work. But then the diarrhea worsened, becoming more severe day by day. By the day before yesterday, her condition was extremely dangerous. Consequently, Bao Zhenyuan sent his daughter to Guangren Hospital at 4 p.m. for treatment, but it was ineffective. She died at 6 p.m. The hospital notified the Zhabei Police Station by telephone, ordering detectives Yao Jiaqi and Qiu Sijiu to go and transport Bao's body to the forensic examination office on Fei Lun Road. They investigated the situation and arrested Liu Wang. Yesterday morning, she was escorted to the Criminal Division 1 court of the Special District No. 1. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang explained the situation and charged Liu Wang under Article 306 of the Criminal Code, stating that the case required a forensic examination this morning. Therefore, he requested that the case be adjourned. Liu Wang confessed to performing the abortion on the deceased but claimed that the cause of death was due to the deceased's own negligence in diet. Criminal Division Chief Qian Hongye reviewed the confession and ordered that the case be adjourned for further hearing. Liu Wang was granted bail of five hundred yuan due to her old age, but if no bail was provided, she would be detained. At 10 a.m., Prosecutor Tang from the Special District No. 1 Prosecutor's Office arrived to examine the body. Bao Zhenyuan stated that he did not know beforehand that his daughter was going to get an abortion. Detective Qiu then submitted a report detailing the investigation into Bao's affair with someone. Mr. Tang then ordered that since Bao Huiying died from illness after an abortion, Liu Wang, who intended to profit by causing an abortion, had already been prosecuted by the police. The body was handed over to Bao Zhenyuan for burial.

Fire Department Builds Giant Fire Engine

—Scheduled to be Commissioned Early Next Month—

Mayor Wu to Be Invited to Officiate at the Commissioning Ceremony, Assigned to Caojiadu for Factory Protection

The Shanghai Municipal Police Department Fire Department, in order to expand the city's fire-fighting equipment, has built two of the largest giant pump fire engines, pioneering the self-manufacture of fire pump vehicles in our country. According to the Municipal Police Department Fire Protection Division, one of the vehicles has been completed and tested successfully. The other vehicle is expected to be completed by the end of this month. Mayor Wu is scheduled to preside over the commissioning ceremony in early June. The details are recorded below.

One Vehicle Completed

According to Dong Zhihe, Director of the Municipal Police Department Fire Protection Division, the giant pump truck built by the Fire Department is the largest of all fire engines in our country. Previously, fire trucks in our country were ordered from abroad, each costing more than 20,000 yuan. In order to recover the outflow of profits, two vehicles were self-made, with a total cost of only over 10,000 yuan. One of them, which began manufacturing last winter, has been fully completed after more than three months. The results of the trial yesterday were excellent. Senior officials from the fire brigades in both concessions also visited and expressed satisfaction.

General Equipment

The completed giant fire truck uses imported "Da Meng Tian" brand parts for the engine, while the rest of the equipment uses domestic materials. It has a power of 70 horsepower and a water output of 500 gallons per minute. The vehicle under construction uses a "Carter Lilik" engine with a power of 70 horsepower. It is equipped with a 50-foot high new-style automatic ladder and a hard-pressure pump, with a water output of 350 gallons per minute. It is expected to be completed by the end of this month.

Commissioning Ceremony

It is currently waiting for the completion of the second fire truck. The Caojiadu Fire Brigade has requested the Municipal Police Department to forward a request to Mayor Wu to attend the grand commissioning ceremony at the beginning of next month. The fire truck will be assigned to that area for application. Due to the concentration of factories and the mixture of Chinese and foreign residents in the Caojiadu area, it is necessary to increase fire-fighting capabilities.

Page 13

Successful Experiment in Extracting Casein from Soybean Cake

Invented by Wang Shuheng

Wang Shuheng, a senior in the Chemistry Department of Shanghai University, recognizing that casein is an important raw material for various industries and has been increasingly used in recent years, with annual consumption in various countries being astonishing, noted that the source of casein is extraction from milk, with very low yields. Someone invented extraction from soybeans, with yields far exceeding milk. Now, Mr. Wang has further extracted it from soybean cake, with yields doubling those from soybeans. After a long period of research and experimentation, he has finally succeeded, making a major contribution to the industrial world of our country. Mr. Wang's description is recorded below.

Casein is a protein, with the English name Casein. Milk contains an average of 2.5-3.5%. To this day, all countries in the world rely on this for the extraction of casein. In the past 30 years, the use of casein in industry has become increasingly widespread, and the importance of its manufacturing industry has also increased. Therefore, countries with insufficient milk production must import casein from abroad. For example, Germany imports large quantities of casein from the United States and France, with annual consumption of approximately 15,000,000 pounds. The United States produced only 8,000,000 pounds in 1918, increasing to 18,000,000 pounds in 1927, and importing as much as 28,000,000 pounds from abroad after 1928. The consumption of casein is increasing daily, while the content in milk is so small. Therefore, there is a need to find new sources of supply. Our country's famous major product, soybean, is an ideal item for supplying this new source. Someone has tested extraction, with a maximum yield of 17%, which is six times that of milk. However, the author (Mr. Wang referring to himself) considers that once soybeans are extracted, they can only be used as fertilizer and cannot be pressed for oil again. If it can be extracted from soybean cake, the cost can be reduced several times, so I immediately began research. After a long period of experimentation, the results show that soybean cake not only contains casein, but the content is very high. Each pound of soybean cake can yield more than 160 grams, in other words, the yield accounts for about 36%.

[Manufacturing of Casein in Industry] There are many methods for manufacturing casein in milk, but the large-scale manufacturing methods are no more than the following three: (1) precipitation with acids, (2) coagulation with coagulating enzymes (Rennet), and (3) self-acidifying coagulation. In addition, there is also electrolysis, but this method is extremely difficult in the selection of electrodes and is still in the research stage in the laboratory. It has not yet been applied in industry. The author has conducted multiple experiments on all three methods, and after changing the first method, the results are very good.

[Comparison of Animal Casein and Plant Casein] Casein is a tasteless and odorless white solid. The percentage of its constituent elements is as follows: Casein is a phosphorus-containing protein with a molecular weight of around 1135. It is a weakly acidic salt and forms acid with neutralizing agents. In dilute salt solutions and under Polarized Light, it has a left-handed rotation, is slightly soluble in water, and extremely soluble in caustic soda and concentrated acids, insoluble in alcohol and ethers. If dissolved in strong hydrochloric acid, it produces a beautiful purple color. The above is the commonality of animal casein in milk. The author has performed quantitative analysis of plant casein extracted from soybean cake and compared it with commercially available animal casein (i.e., that extracted from milk), and they are generally similar. Their solubility and chemical effects are also similar.

[Application of Casein in Industry] (1) Various adhesives (Glurd), especially 包·鑲·塗·蓋·Glues (Venneer Glue), (2) artificial hard inlays (Compact), such as Bakelite, Golallth, and artificial horn, (3) photographic film, (4) cosmetics, (5) soap, (6) paper, (7) rayon, (8) artificial leather, (9) wallpaper, (10) paint, (11) pharmaceuticals, (12) food, (13) electrical insulators, (14) shoe polish, (15) massage cream, (16) mineral oil coagulants, (17) waterproof cloth, (18) insecticide powder, (19) dyeing industry, (20) refining alcohol. From this, it can be seen that casein is truly one of the promising new industries in our country. Given the important position of soybeans in our country today, this industry truly needs to be developed.

(2) A pine and cypress archway will be erected in front of the gate, and Yuan Hongjun will be appointed to contact the flower and tree industry and the bamboo industry associations on behalf of the group. The Plight of the China Merchants Inland River Shipping Bureau

The China Merchants Bureau's inland river routes consist of fifteen lines, nineteen small steamers, sixteen company ships, and four cargo ships, operating in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. In 1930, the National China Merchants Bureau leased them to the Zhejiang Construction Department. In June 1931, they were subleased to businessman Zhang Jingpei, under the name of the China Merchants Inland River Shipping Bureau Management Office, for a term of four years, with an annual rent of 30,800 yuan. The affiliated routes were contracted out to local shipping merchants one after another, with annual rental income of approximately 80,000 yuan. The payment of rent to the Zhejiang Construction Department and the expenses for repairing ships, as well as room rent, salaries, and all miscellaneous expenses, totaled more than 78,000 yuan. From July 1931 to the estimated budget for 1933, income and expenses could still be offset. However, during the Shanghai war, as many as thirteen small steamers were requisitioned for military use. After the ceasefire, when the ships were recovered, they were all severely damaged, with repair costs and compensation for food and labor losses exceeding 20,000 yuan. Recently, with the gradual completion of highways in various counties in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and the competition from declining automobile prices, the inland river shipping industry has plummeted. Although lines such as Xili, Suqin, and Suhang are bound by contracts, the rent has been reduced again and again, to less than half of the original contracted price. The Xicheng line has even disappeared in effect. Therefore, the total income has been reduced to more than 47,000 yuan. In 1934, due to drought and water depletion, navigation was suspended for three months. Although various expenses were extremely frugally managed, the losses were still significant. The lessee reluctantly maintained due to contractual constraints. However, the contractors of each route have long requested to terminate the contracts and return the leases one after another. When the contract expires in the future, the rental income is feared to be less than 40,000 yuan, and the age of the ships is increasing, requiring even greater repairs. After the lease term expires, it may be difficult to continue.

Kang Yuan Canning Factory Implements Group Wedding System

In recent years, extravagant customs have prevailed, and the marriages of men and women often follow superficial trends. Occasionally, those who care about the world advocate frugality or practice it themselves. Although it is temporarily praised, few respond, and the effect is minimal. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal Government has stipulated the Shanghai New Life Group Wedding Method, eliminating all the cumbersome formalities of the secular world. The solemnity and seriousness of the ceremony are very suitable for holding a wedding. Xiang Kangyuan, the general manager of the Kang Yuan Canning Factory in this city, has always taken it as his mission to promote frugality and enhance social welfare. He extremely agrees with the group wedding method. On the ninth of this month, he convened a general meeting of all employees to explain the benefits and necessity of frugality. The listeners were moved. He also proposed a method for employees of the factory to participate in group weddings, divided into two types: those held in the municipal government and those held in the factory. All those who live in the city or plan to live in Shanghai with their families after marriage must apply to participate and should strive for frugality and not host banquets. Those who wish to go to the municipal government will be given twenty yuan for participation fees by the factory. For those who wish to hold weddings at the factory, the factory will reserve a date every two months, decorate the auditorium, prepare marriage certificates, provide refreshments, and invite the associate manager to be the wedding officiant. All expenses will be borne by the factory. If anyone is wealthy or constrained by circumstances and cannot comply, they must first donate three months' salary. Those who deliberately disobey and are unwilling to comply will have four months' salary deducted, all of which will be allocated to charitable expenses. The proposal was voted on at the general meeting and unanimously approved. Rules were immediately drafted, announced, and implemented. It is also heard that in order to promote frugality, if any colleagues have weddings or funerals, they should not send out wedding invitations or obituaries within the factory. They can report to the personnel department, which will announce on their behalf. Colleagues who give gifts are limited to one yuan from superiors to subordinates, four jiao from subordinates to superiors, and six jiao for peers. Only reduction is allowed, not exceeding the limit. The company's promotion of frugality and reduction of the pain of living is truly enough to criticize the prevailing customs and cultivate virtues, which is commendable.

Special Publication

Discussion on Sino-Japanese Economic Cooperation (6th continuation)

— Mu Ouchu

The five fundamental principles are:

(1) Negatively, the real intention of economic control by the strong over the weak should not be disguised under the beautiful name of "economic cooperation" or adjustment. At the same time, positively, the principle of equal and mutually beneficial reciprocity should be adopted.

(2) Negatively, the name of economic adjustment should not be used as a means of political movements against China or against countries other than China; at the same time, positively, economic mutual benefit and the mutual assistance of management and production technologies should be grasped.

(3) Negatively, it should not include any form of current loans and credit settings, and the above-mentioned loan of the difference between import and export prices; at the same time, positively, in the new agreements or joint economic or financial organizations arising from Sino-Japanese economic adjustment, both China and Japan should be able to enjoy complete equity, equal opportunity.

(4) Negatively, the so-called eradication of "anti-Japanese" or "anti-Japanese goods" (which is actually a national goods movement) should not be linked to Sino-Japanese economic adjustment; at the same time, positively, the Japanese side should respect the Chinese side's national goods promotion movement.

(5) Negatively, it should not be publicized that the current economic depression in China is due to the rejection of Japanese goods, and it should be recognized that Sino-Japanese economic adjustment is only a way for both China and Japan to relieve their respective national difficulties.

These two premises and five principles, although not the entirety of the conditions for Sino-Japanese economic adjustment, can be said to be the minimum requirements. If the Japanese side can follow them, then the future of Sino-Japanese economic adjustment is bright. However, when we hear about the Greater East Asia Co-Prosperity Sphere economy that Japan is advocating, we can't help but feel worried. In other words, if a Sino-Japanese "Manchuria" group economy is implemented under the leadership of Japan, it is necessary to pay careful attention. Moreover, this group economy is to make China and the puppet organizations equally subject to Japanese control, and we can see this kind of ambition in many Japanese speeches. Moreover, in the current complex international situation, Japan is urgently needed to form a Greater East Asia Co-Prosperity Sphere economy in order to open up its way of survival and to prepare for the Second World War. If we do not understand this point and echo the empty words of Sino-Japanese economic adjustment, it is tantamount to voluntarily joining Japan's Sino-Japanese "Manchuria" group economy and being arbitrarily controlled by Japan. We are not opposed to Sino-Japanese economic adjustment. If Sino-Japanese economic adjustment is indeed beneficial to China's national economy and people's livelihood, we will support it without hesitation. Otherwise, we dare not support it. We believe that the issue of Sino-Japanese economic adjustment is an extremely serious political issue that cannot be ignored, and it is a major issue related to China's survival. Therefore, we sincerely call on people across the country to earnestly study and pay attention to this issue!
