Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Emperor Unemployment Insurance

— Qiong Sheng

Since the King of Siam failed in his power struggle with the parliament, he immediately announced his abdication and lived a "Siam Overseas Chinese" life in London. After his nephew Ananda succeeded to the throne, the general public and officials did not have the same "loyal heart" as our "social" doctors when they saw Puyi, so we have not heard any talk about giving the King of Siam, who used to be rich in the entire country, an annual salary of 5 million yuan to show the benevolence of the descendants of the Yellow Emperor. Therefore, the King of Siam, who once called himself an orphan and was rich throughout the country, is now alone in a foreign land, taking refuge in another country, which makes people think of "the unbearable memories of the old country."

However, this imagination is an overestimation. Perhaps he cannot sell "antiques" such as precious pearls and dragon-eye pearls like the Manchu Qing imperial family, but the 20th century can make him smarter. After "retirement," he can receive 40,000 US dollars a year in unemployment insurance. Because a Paris dispatch said: The King of Siam, aware of the many kings of various countries who have lost their thrones, took out unemployment insurance for one million US dollars from British and French insurance companies a few years ago. When Ananda succeeded to the throne, he had already received compensation from the insurance company. In the future, he will receive a net of 40,000 US dollars per year until the end of his days.

When a person becomes a king and is the only one to be respected, he will naturally develop a psychology of "I am the country." In addition, in a situation where "all the land under the heavens is the king's land, and all the people on the land are the king's subjects," indeed no one wants to "be a king for all generations." Enjoying endless glory and wealth, wearing endless brocade and silk, and eating endless jade rice and golden waves, how could there be such a person who would willingly give up the "unified country" to others so easily? If you want to give it, unless you kill yourself. Therefore, it is rare and not easy for an emperor to become "unemployed."

Tea Market

— Ye Fei

"Small tea leaves... She Du... Bridge above... Come..." The old man's voice echoed through the tea merchants' row; outside the doors of Wan Yuan and Xiang Tai, several mountain goods shops, were already posted signs saying, "Morning and evening prices differ; a single price is set now." Villagers rushing to the early market passed the shop entrances, their hearts feeling much lighter than usual; so, they gathered around, some asking the shop owners about tea prices, some standing by watching the signs. Seeing the notice, "This shop's small tea leaves will be weighed and priced starting tomorrow," they swallowed, temporarily suppressing the hunger in their bellies, and a gleam of hope gradually appeared in their once lifeless eyes.

In the town of Xia Gang, the boats collecting "Qing Tou" (tender tea leaves) from Dongshan were crowded together, one after another. Several of the plump faces of the mountain goods shop owners revealed a hint of smug smiles. Wan Yuan Shan, especially, swaying his large head, his tiny eyes almost squinting into slits, grinned and chatted with the "Pai Yuan" households at the shop entrance:

"Hey! This spring is cold, the yield will probably be small!"

"Isn't that right? The tea trees only have sprouts now; you might need glasses to find a few tea leaves!" Crab Claw Four chimed in.

"But now people are waiting for money, have nothing to eat, even the finest ones will be picked; as long as the shops weigh..." Crooked Head Jin Bin said thoughtfully.

"That's right! Crab Claw Four, you should pay attention to the tea-making this year, don't let it be like last year, either too damp or so dry it turns to powder."

"Yes, boss! This year I'll have to fire the wok myself; women's hands are delicate and afraid of pain, so it won't do in the end; but will the market be better this year?" Crab Claw Four originally came to inquire about prices.

"That's hard to say; you see, even after Qingming Festival, not many tea merchants have come." Wan Yuan Shan stroked his short, eight-shaped mustache and replied with experience.

"Probably two jiao entering customs is unlikely, last year it was more than two jiao per tael! At the beginning, I even sold it for three jiao per tael."

Crab Claw Four left the shop entrance, looked around at the teahouses and taverns, and saw that everyone had left, even Crooked Head Jin Bin and Hanged Silver Dragon had gone home to eat. So, he hung his damp pipe on his arm and walked home.

He thought, even if he sold cheaply last year, he still got two jiao. If this year doesn't reach last year's price, then the villagers might have to eat river water. In the past, one season of tea leaves was a small income, and the silkworm raising capital had to follow its lead; silkworm raising was the big hope, the living expenses from May to August all depended on it, "A desolate spring, three bitter months, eight months of hardship," if there weren't these two seasons of income, how would the villagers get by? But now, silkworm raising is already a difficult topic, so this season's small income is our only life-saving Bodhisattva. However, in recent years, the tea trade with foreign firms is not smooth; the Japanese, the Russians, they also know how to grow tea; it's really possible that this bowl of rice will be taken away in the future!

Crab Claw Four walked and thought, and when he got home, he saw that the door was locked, knowing that his wife had already eaten and gone to the mountain to pick tea leaves; a key was hidden in a wall hole, a secret known only to him and her, no one else knew. He opened the wok lid, saw that it was soybean porridge for dinner, and without a choice ate two large bowls, then went to the mountain to pick tea leaves with his wife.

This year, the spring started late, so the tea leaves sprouted late too. The sprouts on the tea trees were really only the size of rice grains now; it took effort to pick an ounce of "Qing Tou," and one ounce of dried tea leaves required three ounces of "Qing Tou." The two of them picked from morning till dark, barely managing to gather a wokful, weighing less than four ounces of dried tea leaves.

The next morning, Crab Claw Four took a small package of tea leaves to the tea market. He saw that there were many people, but they were all small farm households; there weren't even half a jin households. The entrance to Xiang Tai shop was also packed, making the street much livelier than usual.

He walked into Wan Yuan shop, only to see Wan Yuan Shan was so busy that he could barely breathe while weighing tea leaves.

"These tea leaves are too dark; they're only worth one and a half jiao per tael!"

"Ah! The fire was too strong; it's already burnt. Two taels and four qian, three and a half jiao."

"Eh! There are too many white leaves here; four and a half taels, deduct five qian for the wrapping paper, five jiao big money."

"..."

He watched them weigh one package after another; they either said it was too damp or too dry, there were hardly any good ones. He didn't seem to hear the sound of "Shop owner, add some!" as he opened one package and went to weigh the second: "Sell it if you want, don't sell it if you don't!"

"Is the price really much worse than last year?" Crab Claw Four was a bit doubtful. "It can't be!"

Rural Sketch

Slow down, father, mother asked you to buy five copper coins' worth of soy sauce.

Square and Circle

— Xiao Ying

In this ancient country of ours on the continent of East Asia, we have always been considered the "sick man." The acquisition of this fine name is naturally not a recent event, and naturally it has its considerable factors. Although now, thanks to the urgent calls of those who care, there has been some progress overall, enough to attract a little attention, but after all, because its latent power is too great, wanting to save this established reputation is by no means something that can be done in the shortest amount of time.

Recently, the tuberculosis test of elementary school students in this city, when the results met with us, could not help but generate a kind of emotion. Although only five schools participated, but judging from the statistics, those infected with lung disease actually account for more than 70 percent. This is worth noting.

Children are sprouting seedlings. If they are not properly cultivated when they are "sprouting," then their growth is bound to be very dangerous, and maybe even die halfway.

Therefore, we believe that in addition to "self-healing," in addition to parents needing to pay close attention, the establishment of children's sanatoriums is indeed essential!

"In recent years, the social economy has been very sluggish," this statement can always be heard often, whether in the newspapers or on people's lips. And after hearing it, what then? Some are "silent," some "respond with a faint smile," and some are "filled with emotion." Although these things don't have any practical effect, what else can you expect them to do?

People in the "social circle" cried, jumped, and even wept in this atmosphere, but people outside the circle are still laughing, comfort has blinded their hearts, as if that sharp circle will never be related to them. However, infants who don't understand human affairs, although they have no part in either circle, cannot escape the net of this circle, and must endure the refinement of the atmosphere. For this, they can only hate being born in a bad year, there is nothing else to say.

Thus, infants who have just left the womb are painfully sent to "infant asylums," painfully allowed to be "adopted" by others, painfully separated from the affection of both sides.

In the modern era where males dominate the center of society, the concept of "valuing men" is always unavoidable in the eyes of the general public. Thus, in the past, infants in infant asylums could often be taken away in a dozen days, but now? Because of the high tide of the atmosphere, it has reached the point of "no one caring" and feeling "overcrowding." Here, one cannot help but let out a long sigh and think to oneself: "In recent years, the social economy has been very sluggish."

Random Notes of a Wanderer

— Ke Ming

Around noon, the boat stopped at the small ferry of Sandao Kou. The boatman tied the rope, and the passengers inside the cabin began to stir: men carrying packages and baskets, women leading children, like a string of fish, walked to the bow of the boat, to the gangplank, to the shore, to the dry little road—there, perhaps there was a nest-like old home, perhaps there was warm friendship, perhaps a fire-like irresistible love was burning... Thus, a string of people, people living under different circumstances—there were retired old soldiers, middle-aged men wandering the world selling skills under the banner of "making friends through martial arts," men working as servants in big mansions in Shanghai, people ringing bells and setting up stalls on the street "reading faces," and wanderers who had forgotten the term "home"—went to different roads with different purposes.

The boatman lay down on the deck at the bow of the boat, which was covered with bright sunshine. He counted the collected boat money, bundling two strings of cash together; but after working hard rowing for a trip, he only made about twenty strings, and everything is not thriving this year, it's really hard for those who work hard to make ends meet to get enough to eat.

Thinking about it, he sighed; a kind of fear, like a misty fog, shifted in the wrinkles on his forehead beyond five thousand. —Ah, what kind of days are these?

Sitting up, he packed a pipe with damp tobacco and smoked, the shore was quiet, and there weren't many ripples in the water. The thoughts of a young man bloomed like rapeseed flowers, carrying a golden posture, opening up in the garden of memory. At that time, there was no suffering, no worry, life itself was as quiet as the spring pool, the summer night, and the autumn wheat ears.

It has already been a very, very long time.

Father was a dark, strong man, but he was also very honest, unable to argue with people in more than three sentences, the veins on his face would all swell up in anxiety, but people didn't dare to argue with him; he didn't have an amazing mouth, but he did have strong fists. Taking the woman, using the boat as a home, he ventured out from one wharf to another.

I love the water, I love the sea—I like to watch the ferocious waves in the sea, and the sun, like a fire plate, floating at the end of the horizon. Was I born and raised as a wanderer in the water town?

So, I grew up. But I also don't lack the body of a strong young man. Helping the guys row the scull, not even uttering a word of fatigue for most of the day.

The old man praised as he looked me over with my dark big eyes, saying: Good fellow, you really grew up in the water town, a seed of wandering. So he used the old sailor's wildness, patting my broad shoulders: "Hey, I say, young man, you should find a pretty young lady to be your companion."

The older generation gradually weakened, fell down, and along with the youth of the old men, these peaceful days will also pass forever and will never come again. When I used my powerful arms to take over the boat (the wandering, drifting home) from the old man's hands, the old era had already shed a layer of its shell; and the new wandering also began at this moment.

Thus: one oar after another, one port after another, one river after another, one year after another, when the labor of people has become a commodity in the auction market, it has unknowingly drifted by day after day.

—The water town is our birthplace, the water town is our grave, we are innate wanderers.

It was noon, the crew brought out the meal, and in the hot rice fragrance, someone on the shore shouted:

—Hey, the boat is coming!

I hurriedly put on a smiling face to greet them, thinking: I don't know where the dream of tomorrow midnight will be lost.

Page 21

Spring Arrives in the World

— Mian Huai (Cherishing Memories)

Spring has finally adorned this gray world.

The window of the writing room faces south. With tired eyes, as if from a hangover, I squander the bright spring sunshine in Arabic numerals. Although the sunlight, like a mother's love, caresses my desk very early, it makes me feel even more weary of life. Spring is a season of vigor: grass and trees return to life, hibernating insects wriggle, and the flags waving in the light breeze, advertising big sales, also hide the rampant tide of recession around the world. Even the most unambitious humans raise the creed that "the plan of the year lies in spring," as if trying hard to do more things. But this separation of a layer of glass window, in my view, is as far away as another planet!

Young people shouldn't have such thoughts! That loud voice thundered in my ears. Really? In such doubt, I made a phone call to my friend. I said: "It's spring, come to my house on Sunday. Let's play some tricks from our student days. Anything is fine. We must spend this day in the most satisfying way."

On the expecting morning, I got up early, wiped the windows, and swept the floor. When I saw the sun gently slipping into the well, I cheered. It wasn't she who adorned this gray world, it was the world's natural light.

I took the newspaper delivered that day and sat alone in the small patio, facing east, flipping through the supplement as if fighting for it in the reading room. The pieces of advertisements were all jumping, every lead character had changed to "Spring has arrived!" So I threw the newspaper into the corner of the wall, mindful that my friend hadn't changed his habit of sleeping late from school days. I calculated how to send this sun to the west mountain in a satisfying way. Watching the clock, it was still early. I knew that waiting for the arrival of a happy day should deliberately do some things that one doesn't want to do, so that when it suddenly arrives, it will be a hundred times more interesting.

So I returned to the bedroom to tidy up my desk, newspapers, magazines, almond extract, aspirin, arranging them in the most orderly way. I wiped the dust off the photo frame, and when I was whistling unconsciously, my friend pushed the door in. But unexpectedly, I didn't feel a hundred times more interesting. He took off his long coat, sat down, and hurriedly started smoking.

After a long while, he said that he was called to the company to do some things that shouldn't have been done today. Remembering your appointment, I wanted to finish it hastily but was supervised by foreigners. He ended the following words with a sigh.

This small blow hasn't completely suppressed our enthusiasm. After lunch, we discussed a list of how to spend the day. We always felt that the tricks we played in our student days seemed too boring now. And the interesting things? No one had that idea hidden in their heads?

We sent the sun back to the west mountain without leaving the bedroom a step. I remember we talked about many old classmates, someone left home and traveled far away, someone lost their job, someone's marriage was unhappy... And strangely, our lives are exactly what so-and-so wants the most. I looked out the window, and the sun outside that layer of glass gradually left my sight.

Opening Chapter "Shou Tu" (Receiving Vomit)

Jade beauty's singing and dancing has not returned, lonely Qin Tower, cold emerald terrace, the mirror has not been put away, listening to the sounds of drums through the night, lazily, lingering, happily seeing the courtesan returning drunk, cheeks red with wine, helpless emerald sleeves falling, maids supporting her, delicate and powerless, beautiful and resentful, head lazy to raise, the nanny happily calling there is a guest, the beauty is drunk and cannot accompany, going to the bed, starry eyes blurry, Qin Zhong is a long night companion in the boudoir, immediately taking a towel to personally receive the vomit, calling for tea and following with a cup, the golden rooster awakens the wandering immortals, asking who is the gentleman, the little lady must not buy the oil name Qin Zhong, last spring admiring the talent, accumulating flower silver for a good meeting, happened to meet returning drunk last night, offering tea to receive the vomit personally, quickly taking clothes to wipe is me, the beauty hearing this said it is rare, boldly thanking the talent, carefully inquiring when will we meet again.

Classical Prose

Wang Bingmei Donglai Bo Yi

On the Use of Troops

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

The gentleman uses troops with sincerity. There is nowhere sincerity is not used. The world has not yet seen sincerity and lightness. Though the enemy seeks to entice him, how can he be enticed? The world has not yet seen sincerity and greed. Though the enemy seeks to bait him, how can he be baited? The world has not yet seen sincerity and disorder. Though the enemy seeks to confuse him, how can he be confused? Using this sincerity to comfort and govern, the masses will not doubt. It cannot be confused by counter-questioning. Using this sincerity to prepare and defend, the masses will not be idle. It cannot be misled by cunning schemes. That which they used to gain victory, was because of lightness. Once sincerity is established, the five vices are all eliminated. Even if the ancient experts of war encircled and attacked, exhausting their cunning plans a hundred or a thousand times, the gentleman treats them with sincerity alone. Their cunning is exhausted by ten thousand but not enough, my sincerity guards one and is more than enough. They are always labored and I am always at ease. They are always moving and I am always still. Using ease to control labor, using stillness to control movement, is this not the way to constant victory in the world? Therefore, those who discuss the excellence of using troops in the world, are surely none other than the gentleman.

Shen Bao This Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

New Developments in 1935 Model Automobiles

— Translated by Qin

This article is from the 72nd volume, 2nd issue of "Automobile Industry." It was written by an American automotive engineering expert, P.M. Heldt. It thoroughly elaborates on the areas of improvement in new cars. Therefore, I translated it as follows:

Those who have visited the New York Auto Show generally believe that there have been significant changes in automobile design in the past year. In reality, these changes are only on the surface. Everything inside, under the hood, and under the car body is pretty much the same as last year. Except for one thing: the redistribution of weight to increase driving stability. However, there are also many minor improvements.

In the past, the greatest efforts of the engineering department were spent on sheet metal work to increase sales demand. As a result, "streamlining" has become almost a buzzword. The most important and most common reform is to hide the spare tire in the rear of the car body. This allows the car body to gradually approach a true streamlined shape. Fender skirts and rear panels have also been greatly improved in form compared to previous tilted fenders and other protruding parts, minimizing their air resistance.

Almost many automobile designers believe that if the shape of a car is truly close to a theoretical streamlined shape, then the car body will be ridiculed for having a large nose. This is naturally not welcome by customers. Therefore, they came up with a method to streamline each part of the car separately, making their shape the most suitable and most attractive. The merging of the radiator grille and the hood must also match the fenders. Then, connect the parts and use sheet metal fairings to create the streamlined shape of an airplane wing.

Here, whether it is people in the automobile industry or the general public who use automobiles, they cannot help but be extremely curious about the independent front suspension. They don't know how American automakers will implement this independent front suspension system after their first year of testing. If an automobile manufacturer has a standard for the manufacturing program of the next year, then he will definitely be able to make his test satisfactory. Several manufacturers who adopted this system last year have generally not changed it this year. In addition, two new manufacturers have also adopted this system. At the same time, some manufacturers do not use this system, perhaps because of its higher price.

Everyone also knows that independent front suspension is indeed more expensive to manufacture when installed on American cars. Buyers generally have a deep impression that there are two different types of cars on the market now. Their prices are different. The more expensive ones are equipped with independent front suspension, while others are not.

Before the independent front suspension was fully developed, another change began last year to improve driving comfort. This is the movement of the engine part forward and the increase of the front suspension's range of motion. In the past, the radiator was always placed above the front axle. The engine was further back so that its position could be lowered without interfering with the front axle. This year, the engine is mostly moved forward between six and eight inches. This not only reduces shock and noise, but also allows the seats in the car to move forward at the same time, away from the rear axle, so that passengers are not subjected to the vibration transmitted from the rear wheels. This also makes it easier to streamline the rear of the car body. At the same time, it can hide the spare tire in the back of the car body.

The engines are also more powerful than last year's. This is due to the increased intake volume and compression ratio, not relying on increasing the displacement of the pistons. We can try to make the compression ratio higher and higher every day, but still not make the engine prone to knocking. The cylinder heads made of cast iron can have a compression ratio of up to 6.5 or even 6.7. However, since we adopted aluminum, it has been found in recent years that its ratio is too large. Although recent improvements in combustion chambers can also increase horsepower, there probably won't be rapid development without improvements in the anti-knock properties of fuel. As for installing a heat regulator in the intake manifold to adjust the heat, it also helps to increase horsepower.

In addition, the timing of the spark is a big problem in increasing the compression ratio. In places with a very high ratio, we probably use the vacuum in the intake manifold to control the spark. When the engine is running slowly due to heavy load, the spark is very delayed, preventing all the effects of high pressure, such as explosions.

The average standard compression ratio used in passenger cars last year was from 5.72 to 5.94.

Because we want to increase the compression ratio, the volume of the compression chamber has to be reduced, and difficulties arise with the clearance next to the valves, especially for L-head engines. In the past year, a lot of research has been spent on this to give the compression chamber a suitable shape that does not hinder the flow of gas. We already know that at high altitudes, exhaust is easier to solve than intake, and exhaust valves can be made smaller than intake valves. For the same reason, the clearance next to the exhaust valve can also be less than the intake valve. Using this theory when designing the combustion chamber, the intake volume of the intake system can be increased, and the volumetric efficiency of the engine can also be improved at high speeds. Not only that, increasing the ratio of the exhaust valve area to the volume can make exhaust gas easier to cool and avoid the tendency to explode.

The gradual increase in horsepower has made the cylinder need a very effective cooling system, especially at the exhaust valve seat. There are currently two methods. One method is to install a water distributor in the water jacket to spray water onto the wall of the exhaust valve. The other method is to extend the water jacket to the crankcase. The former benefits can reduce the temperature of the exhaust valve seat, reduce the damage to the valve seat, and prevent the valve from gradually sinking. The latter benefit can reduce the temperature of the oil in the crankcase, protecting its vulnerable parts from damage even under extremely severe working conditions.

The bearing load also increases with the increase in speed. Therefore, sometimes the safety factors used seem to be no longer applicable. Therefore, the crankshaft has more complete weight balancing in many places to reduce the load on the main bearings. The most heavily loaded bearing in the engine—apart from the piston pin, because the friction damage inside is not great—can be considered the crankshaft pin bearing. Now, two types of passenger cars use a bronze with a very high lead content to make this bearing. There is also a type of car that uses an alloy of cadmium, silver, and copper to make the bearing. This alloy has properties similar to leaded bronze, has a very high melting point, and does not lose its strength at high temperatures.

Aluminum cylinders are used more widely, although one manufacturer has abandoned this method due to cost considerations. In addition, in the past five years, automotive mechanical equipment has been able to produce more improvements in driving comfort, convenience, and economy. Manufacturers have determined that standard equipment. It is very obvious that in the past seven years, even in extremely difficult times, manufacturers have been actively seeking to improve equipment in order to facilitate sales. But this year, the situation is different. Many manufacturers have abandoned some of the equipment that was considered standard last year. The reason is the increase in manufacturing costs and the reduction in external purchasing power.

There have not been major changes to carburetor equipment. Down-draft carburetors are now almost the equipment adopted worldwide. Air filters and intake silencers are also widely used. Dual carburetors are now used on many eight-cylinder engines, whether V-shaped or inline. Many manufacturers now also move the spark coil to the engine. This can reduce the length of the high-voltage wires, radio isolation can be easier, and it is also beneficial for ignition.

Everyone has also paid considerable attention to the engine's lubrication system. On at least two types of engines, the gauge port has been adopted on the crankshaft. The advantage is that the oil delivery rate is not affected by the bearing clearance. Therefore, it has nothing to do with the gradual wear of the parts. Our pure experience tells us that after a car has traveled a certain mileage, it is often difficult for the lubricating oil to maintain a sufficient pressure. But this difficulty has now been solved by the gauge port. In addition, there is a new development: the use of larger oil pumps and oil passages. The disadvantage is that it makes it difficult for the lubricating oil to supply the normal amount of oil when the car is just started. The Packard car has a removable oil filter that can change the oil pressure to automatically clean the oil filter's intermediate products. The Chevrolet car adds an oil injector to lubricate the crankshaft pin bearings. The lubricating oil is injected into the connecting rod holes, and the pressure varies with the driving speed.

The capacity of the generator has also increased. But its size has not increased. The weight does not increase either. We only need to add a fan. At the same time, increase its speed within the possible range. The generator on the Packard car can supply 30 amps of current. But this also has a disadvantage: it is easy to overcharge the battery and cause damage. Therefore, the new model also has a protective relay.

Many problems occur with the gearbox. The reason is that the horsepower of the primary engine gradually increases, but the size of the gearbox does not change. Secondly, in recent years, we have strived for convenience in management, and there have been many changes. There are two ways to deal with these problems. (1) Increase the mechanical advantages of the gearbox. This is to increase the stroke of the gearbox pedal, which seems uneconomical. (2) Reduce the pressure on the gearbox plate. Therefore, the spare capacity is reduced. However, this will inevitably cause the gearbox to slip, causing heat and wear. To avoid this difficulty, we now use ventilation methods. Its vents have air filter screens to prevent dust from entering.

There is also a new type of semi-centrifugal gearbox. It is equipped with one or a row of springs, using its lighter pressure to transmit the machine's maximum torque.

Finally. Speaking of braking systems, hydraulic brakes are very fashionable. In the past, the emergency brake on the propeller shaft was always connected to the hydraulic brake, but now that we use the brake lever, we can save an emergency brake. In addition, there is a vacuum power brake adopted by Heber. However, Chrysler has abandoned this type of braking system.

Review of Road Safety Issues

— Ying Dai

(1) Progress in Safety

Currently, the most serious problem regarding automobiles is to reduce the number of accidents on the roads. Perhaps no one would deny this. Therefore, people who use the roads should be responsible for solving this problem, so that the number of accidents can be effectively reduced. Before we notice that the number of cars traveling on the roads is increasing day by day, although we will know that automobile accidents are only increasing and decreasing according to weekly and monthly investigation records. However, automobile manufacturing is currently more advanced in terms of safety than in the past, even than a few years ago. No one would deny this. According to various records in the United Kingdom, the number of cars traveling on the roads has generally increased by 9.4% in the past three years. However, the number of people killed or injured in accidents has only increased by 1%. If this method of comparison is based on the mileage traveled by automobiles and the consumption of gasoline, then we can know from the gasoline consumed by automobiles that the number of people killed by automobiles has fallen from 8.71% to 6.67% per million gallons in the past decade.

(2) Road Safety

How exactly does this method of comparison prove the improvement of road safety? It is to combine all the mileage traveled by automobiles and make a statistics with all the automobile injury cases. Then we can get an answer: it is assumed that a car travels 3,000,000 miles per year and will only kill one pedestrian after 430 years of driving. And this statistic is actually estimated to be a bit high. In addition, there is one more thing we should know: the past statistics of automobile homicides did not pay attention to other aspects of influence. However, it has recently been discovered in the United Kingdom that cold easterly winds make it inconvenient for cars to travel. In the same week, the homicide record increased by half compared to normal. The United Kingdom has also proven that deaths caused by poor roads only account for 1.5% of automobile homicide cases. People who are working hard to improve road construction also want to completely eliminate this 1.5% record. The only reason why road safety has improved is that people who use the roads are generally able to take responsibility for prevention and driving automobiles. Surgical treatment has made a lot of progress. And this improvement, traced back to its source, should be attributed to the progress of automobile manufacturing. Currently, the cars you purchase have a lower center of gravity, stronger cross-chassis bars, the effect of counterweight, all-steel body, safety glass, everything is enough to make the safety of passengers increase.

Page 24

(3) Engine Safety

Further speaking, the smoothness of the engine, the use of gears, because of harmonic motion, simple and rapid, the clear indication of stopping or turning, the easy control of headlights, make the control of modern cars by drivers much more convenient than cars a few years ago. Therefore, when driving, drivers do not have to pay too much attention to the handling of the machine, and can concentrate their vision on the road in front of the car and care about safety issues. If we can remember the above advantages, then we can know that the automobile is a very safe type of modern transportation. At the same time. We must not forget that the current driving of automobiles has achieved good results. Everything that was impossible before is now possible. Test drives, anti-skid, and various other cost-consuming and scientific devices are enough to make your car safer and increase its driving value. The increasing development of automobiles. Undoubtedly, any people who drive automobiles should be extra careful to prevent accidents easily due to the increase of vehicles traveling on the road. At the same time. Drivers should also urge automobile manufacturers to strive for perfection in manufacturing to eliminate the ingredients that cause accidents. In this way, the safety level of automobiles will inevitably be improved. The safety and comfort of road travel is a limitless gift. In this era. We know that we are much more advanced than before. But from now on, we should take on more responsibility to make it even more perfect. And to achieve this goal. The most important point. Of course, it lies in reducing the number of accidents. This is something that every traveler should be responsible for promoting.

Daily Inspection and Protection Methods for Automobile Storage Batteries

— Zhen Min

Storage batteries only occupy the position of two kinds of accessories on the entire car. General car owners and drivers often do not pay attention to them. This is really a big mistake. You must know that this small storage battery is actually the central hub for controlling the life of the entire car. The explosion of the engine. The light of the headlights at night. The sound of the horn. Everything depends on the power output of this small storage battery. If the storage battery fails. Then your engine has a very large supply of gasoline. But it will not achieve the purpose of driving. Therefore. When applying storage batteries. We should always inspect and protect them at the specified time. So that it does not produce any obstacles. This is really the responsibility of every driver. Now let's briefly describe the most important points.

(1) Measure Voltage—After the storage battery has been outputting electricity for a long time (about three weeks or more). Its voltage will slowly decrease. At the same time, the current will also become smaller. At this time, you should use a voltmeter (ie, a voltmeter) to measure its short-circuit voltage. (Use the two ends of the meter to really contact the positive and negative electrodes. The time should be short). The voltage after power output should not be less than 1.75 volts. (This refers to ordinary storage batteries used in general cars). Once this limit is reached. You should charge it immediately. Otherwise, sulfuric acid crystals will adhere to the electrode plates. As a result, the entire battery loses its effectiveness.

(2) Injection of Electrolyte—The storage battery causes the electrolyte to gradually evaporate as a result of continuous power output and charging. The ingredients contained in the electrolyte are sulfuric acid and distilled water. Among them, the capacity of sulfuric acid will not decrease. We only allow the addition of distilled water at any time. Make sure that the horizontal line at the top of the electrode plate is completely immersed in the electrolyte.

(3) Precautions for Charging—When the voltage drops to 1.75 volts after power output. You should charge it immediately. But you must pay attention to the following points when charging:

(A) The charging time. Must be at least five hours.

(B) When charging, gas is discharged around the electrodes. This gas is rich in flammability. Do not approach it with fire. To avoid explosion.

(C) Avoid overcharging. Because overcharging can accelerate the evaporation of the electrolyte. At the same time, the metal debris on the electrodes sinks to the bottom of the pool. It is easy to cause a short circuit.

(D) Once the storage battery is weakly powered. You should charge it immediately. Do not leave it for a three-month deadline. (Otherwise, solid sulfuric acid crystals will grow on the electrodes. Destroying the entire battery.

(4) Regulations on Electrolyte Specific Gravity—The specific gravity of the electrolyte. Should have regulations. The highest specific gravity of the electrolyte after charging. Must not exceed 1.300. The low specific gravity after power output. Must not be lower than 1.150. This specific gravity test. A hydrometer can be inserted into the electrolyte to measure it by automatically raising and lowering it.

(5) Precautions for Cleaning Electrolyte—If you want to remove sediment or precipitates from the bottom of the pool. The first step. First, fully charge this storage battery. Then take out the electrode plates. Use distilled water to carefully rinse the electrodes and the surrounding area of the pool. The electrodes should be placed back in their original place when they are not dry. Some storage batteries are equipped with specially made cleaning systems. There is no need to disassemble accessories.

(6) If rust or other phenomena are found on the electrode plate. You should replace it with a new board. To maintain a constant voltage. This replacement of electrode plates. Can be configured to nearby electrical materials.

(7) The two ends of the electrodes should always maintain a conductive state. Apply less Vaseline. To prevent rust.

(8) The vent at the top of the battery. Should always be kept open. Do not allow it to be blocked.

The above are the most important methods of protecting storage batteries. Every driver should always pay attention to them. The batteries used on general cars now. They are all lead-acid storage batteries. Its price is cheaper than Edison storage batteries. However, lead plates are prone to rust and other phenomena. This point must be checked at all times. In order to replace it.

New-style cars now. They all use an electrical machine and battery connection system. After the storage battery is over-powered. It is automatically charged by the generator at any time. The simplicity and speed of this cyclical system. Truly a merit. But sometimes this charging capacity is too weak. We have to use other charging methods.

Austin Adds New Factory

— Fu

Using Electric Keys to Assemble Car Bodies

The Austin Motor Company has recently added a new factory to its Longbridge plant. Using the latest type of conveying machinery. Engaged in assembly work. Its agility and skill are truly amazing. The new factory is worth £20,000. The floor area is 41,000 square feet. It is specially used for car body assembly and its subsidiary work. All Austin car body and chassis combinations. They are all made here. It is estimated that each successful combination only takes one and a half minutes. That is, about 2,000 combinations can be made per week.

This work. Now it is handled by electric keys. Its simplicity is unique. A row of electric keys. Placed on the management platform. The administrator sits in front of the electric keys. In order to preside over the operation of three car body cranes. Each car body. It is lifted from the platform by one of the three cranes. After turning and dispatching. After adjusting its position. Slowly placed on top of the chassis. It fits perfectly. Not a millimeter off. The accuracy of its coordination. Truly has the magic of nature. As for the matched chassis. It is also newly transported from the shipping point. Wait for the car body to be assembled in seconds. The car has been assembled. Waiting to be subjected to the final steps. Then it is moved away by the conveying rope. This automobile conveying rope. It is a total of six. Each is 100 yards long. Two of them. There are also high-rise parts. Allowing mechanics to work under passing cars. As for the various parts required for the conveying rope. And various necessary equipment. It is supplied by three mezzanine supply points. And the three supply points. A conveyor with a length of about 600 yards is used. Get supplies from the main supply point. Therefore, in the entire factory. No matter when and where. All component parts needed for the transport machine. All are automatically supplied. Furthermore, at the end of each conveying rope. Equipped with electric gasoline pumps. Quickly provide fuel to the Austin. Therefore, each car can be driven with its own power after being assembled. In order to test it.

Overview of the New 1935 Oldsmobile

— Yun

The 1935 Oldsmobile six-cylinder and straight-eight-cylinder new cars have now been presented to the world. The new cars are even more spacious and grand than before. They not only possess all the mechanical engineering advancements of 1934, but also have several new important features. The first major improvement of the new car that should be mentioned is the Fisher body. The newly installed roof is pressed from a solid, seamless steel plate and is closely integrated with the body, as if it were a single part. Passengers inside the car are assured of robust and excellent steel for their safety, whether above, below, or in any other direction. As for the streamlined design, it makes the whole car graceful, magnificent, and extremely attractive. This is mainly due to the new radiator cap and the rear bumper, which can thoroughly achieve streamlining.

The new car adopts an X-type frame, whose strength and solidity have increased by 40% compared to previous models. The chassis, engine, and body all use sound-absorbing and perfect organization. The interior of the car is spacious, with greatly increased head and leg room. The seats are wider and the padding is excellent. The spacious luggage compartment and the redistribution of the entire car's weight mean that all passengers are now positioned between the axles, making them feel particularly comfortable. This advantage is due to the fact that the motor and seats of the new car are positioned about five inches further forward than the 1934 model.

Whether it is the six-cylinder or eight-cylinder model, the new car has a longer wheelbase. The increase in its original power is mostly due to the use of a newly designed cylinder head, which has a higher compression ratio and can still use standard fuel. The intake manifold system and carburetor have been greatly improved, making their use more economical and cost-effective. According to actual road tests, the six-cylinder car achieves 18 miles per gallon at a speed of 50 miles per hour.

There are seven body styles available for both the six-cylinder and eight-cylinder models. The horsepower of the six-cylinder model is 84 to 90 horsepower, while the eight-cylinder model is 90 to 100 horsepower. The engine adopts a new three-point suspension method, and the operation is quieter than before. Therefore, whether in terms of efficiency, economy, comfort, aesthetics, or any other aspect, the new car has made great progress.

Supplement to the *Shen Bao* (Shanghai News), Local Edition: Movie Special

A Psychological Analysis of Ruan Lingyu's Suicide

— Bo Ning

Love affairs are not uncommon in the film industry. Hollywood sees dozens of scandals every year. Not to mention abroad, there have been quite a few scandalous stories on the domestic film scene that once caused a sensation. Why is it that those people can all live happily, while Ruan Lingyu insisted on quarreling with her own life, resolutely abandoning this world? This must not be accidental; part of it is naturally due to her social background. However, the reporter believes that her personal psychological conditions should be an important factor in her suicide.

Her emotional life... Everyone knows that emotions can determine a person's behavior. You can't ask a melancholy person to dance and prance. You can't ask a happy person to frown and look sad. But people only know that emotions can determine behavior, and they don't know that behavior can also determine emotions. An American psychologist once said, "People don't cry because they are sad, they are sad because they cried; people don't laugh because they are happy, they are happy because they laughed." The films starring Ruan Lingyu, such as "Reminiscences of the Old Capital," "Little Toys," "Life," "The Goddess," and the recent "New Woman," are all social tragedies. Movies are originally plays, and plays are originally just acting, but to make them realistic and moving, the actor must regard the play as part of their own life. This is where the emotional life of the actor is affected. That is, "sad because they cried." This kind of sad emotion in Ruan Lingyu was still latent in normal times and not easy to observe. Once she encountered something unsatisfactory, of course, it would erupt uncontrollably.

Terrible experiences... How do people deal with the environment? Part of it is also determined by past experiences. A Japanese wife, upon seeing her husband, bends down to take off his clogs; an American wife, upon seeing her husband, crosses her legs and asks him to take off her high heels. These are all determined by their past experiences. A Japanese wife would never cross her legs upon seeing her husband, and an American wife would never bend down upon seeing her husband. When Ruan Lingyu lived with Zhang Damin, she once took poison. This was her past experience. Therefore, now that she encountered difficulties, her past experience became active again. Coupled with sad emotions and "strong suggestion," she involuntarily embarked on the old path.

Strong suggestion... When I say a strong suggestion, what is a strong suggestion? Whenever a person has a "pre-existing state," encountering a certain stimulus becomes a strong suggestion. For example, the rickshaw pullers on the road have a "pre-existing state of customers calling for a rickshaw." Anyone who inadvertently raises their hand at the entrance of a theater, they will rush over pulling their rickshaw. Ruan Lingyu already had a past experience of suicide and was awakened by bad emotions and current difficulties. She already had a kind of "pre-existing state of suicide." It is said that when she returned home from the Yangtze Hotel, Ruan had seen two ghosts of impermanence before her death, which was an illusion. And because she has always believed in ghosts, she believed that she was probably "doomed to die" and single-mindedly embarked on the road to death. Alas! Such a promising movie star actually fell for her own psychology, and her life was tragically cut short. It is truly a human tragedy.

The question afterwards... Ruan Lingyu is dead. Apart from sighing, we cannot remedy it. However, she has left behind a serious psychological problem. We know that after Goethe's *The Sorrows of Young Werther* was published, countless young Germans died for love. Suicide also became fashionable in society. Werther is still a fictional character. Ruan Lingyu is a real artist and a figure loved and sympathized with by modern youth. Her death may give young people a "suggestion." Everyone, don't look down on the role of suggestion. Porf. J.M. Baldwin said: "Suggestion is psychological and social." Then we have a responsibility to prevent young men and women. The press, in particular, should pay more attention to this.

Review of "Orawling Death [sic]"

— Ling He

Orawling Death—Paris Screening

Stories like "Tarzan the Ape Man" are almost a myth, but "Crawling Death," which has been translated as "Little Tarzan's Love Story," has a story that is closer to human emotions. This can be seen from the sudden appearance of a black child at that time, because he is completely unrelated to the entire film.

This shows that the author of this film is purely profiting by ignoble methods, so there is also a group of young girls appearing nude. Furthermore, how many animal films can arouse people's interest at present? Although it was a sensation for a time, it is now outdated, let alone a crudely made and vulgar work?

Audience Opinions

My Review of "Serpent Woman"

— Chi Ying

This "Serpent Woman," renamed from "Vortex," is constructed with an extremely ordinary story. From all aspects, there is no miracle worth noting. It gives us some extremely bland images. Its story is based on the evil vortex of the city, which caused a tragic change in a family. So what it tells us is, "People who lack self-control, beware of the evil vortex of the city!"

However, the director neglected the realistic aspects: like Wang Guilin using oversensitive nerves to sigh about the future fate of her son because of the whirlpool of water; Zhang Yi living in a house enjoyed by the middle class with a salary of forty yuan; a socialite who abandons the old and welcomes the new actually falling in love with the proletarian Zhang Yi with the qualities of being tall, brave, and honest. These all seem to be imagined out of thin air.

The director also forgot to introduce the background and life of the socialite. If there were no instructions, it would almost make the audience think she was a dancer. There is also no thorough indication of the evils of the city and the serpentine nature of the beauty. What it shows on the screen is only a part of the fickle socialite.

Zhang Yi is the best among the actors. His resolute performance is commendable. Chen Yanyan's specialty in being lovable is not fully developed here. Wang Guilin and Wang Moqiu can still be called competent. Liu Jiqun's urban gentleman style in a few short scenes is quite experienced.

The first half of the entire play is slightly commendable, but the second half lacks many highlights, such as Zhang Yi's madness after losing favor and the final car speeding. Also, Chen Yanyan waiting for Zhang Yi's return, from dusk to dawn, reflecting the sleeping son, has the flavor of "Madame Butterfly." However, the photography is poor, and the light is too dim.

Some Information about Joan Lowell, the Star of "Heroic Adventure"

— Guo Cheng

Joan Lowell (also the star of the latest Didi Huaxin film "Heroic Adventure") grew up in Berkeley, California. She was the eleventh child in her family. Her mother was a cousin of the poet (James Russell Lowell). Her father was the owner of a small sailing ship. When Joan was only eleven months old, he took her to sea to live on the ship, until she was seventeen years old. In these ten years, she grew up looking like a boy. She already understood all the trivial matters on the ship and was willing to do them. When she was seventeen years old, her father sent her ashore and said to her, "From now on, you should hold the helm of your life and sail on the road of your life."

She ran ashore in ill-fitting clothes and began to try various jobs. She worked like a student who was working and studying at the same time, doing her job during the day and running to night school to study in the evening. She also became a professional swimmer.

She is also able to write. She wrote an amazing adventure novel, "The Cradle of the Deep." After its publication, more than 100,000 copies were sold out in a few weeks, and this book was selected as the best work of the month. This was in April 1929.

Afterwards, Joan Lowell often wrote novels and articles and submitted them to *Cosmopolitan* and *The Saturday Evening Post* for publication, and received countless praises and honors from various groups in society.

She traveled to various places like a newspaper travel reporter. In April 1933, she and her 76-year-old father and two sailors cruised around the world.

She is five feet four inches tall and weighs one hundred and seventeen pounds. She is also an aviator, a skilled equestrian woman, a hunting expert, and a swimming champion. She is proficient in all kinds of sports. She is a rare genius woman.

Mei Lin's Marriage: A World Oddity

Mei Lin, a rising star of Lianhua that is most anticipated by general movie fans, her film "Carefree Gentleman" is of course also a film that people are eagerly looking forward to. We can report to everyone that "Carefree Gentleman" will soon meet with social figures, and Mei Lin has succeeded in this film.

It is naturally a gratifying thing for Mei Lin to succeed in one fell swoop. If we talk about the marriage affairs in the two films "Carefree Gentleman" and "Tian Lun" made by Mei Lin, then it is an extremely ridiculous thing. In "Carefree Gentleman," after she married Han Langan, she married Liu Jiqun again. Now, not long after marrying Han and Liu, she married Zheng Junli again in "Tian Lun." However, her marriage with Zheng Junli in "Tian Lun" was a combination of love, and there was a lot of struggle before marriage. As for her marriage with Han and Liu, even Mei Lin herself did not know how the wedding was held. A woman has gone through two marriages with two men without knowing it herself. Such a thing cannot be said to be a world oddity.

Movie Novel

Anecdotes of the Duke of Wellington (The Iron Duke) (7)

— Xin Zhi

Hope was extinguished, the army collapsed, and Napoleon, like a defeated eagle, immediately fled back to Paris. He fought for a hundred days, which is the famous Hundred Days War in history. His talent and power were certainly no less than before, but fortune was against him, and the general situation was gone. As the saying goes, the collapse of the army is like the collapse of a mountain, and who can save it? The price of Napoleon's hundred days was being exiled to Saint Helena Island.

A month later, the kings and ministers of various countries reconvened the peace conference in Paris to divide the spoils of victory. The Duke of Wellington, as a military man, was not accustomed to the business of weighing the pros and cons, but he was now assigned as one of the ministers. Watching these masters of Europe argue and roar, and contend in the same way as before, he could not help but feel a little contempt. King Louis XVIII of France had now returned to Paris and ascended the throne again. Beside him still stood the daughter of Marie Antoinette, arrogant and domineering, and wanting to monopolize national power like her mother. Outside Louis' bedroom, the Duke of Wellington paced back and forth, his heart in a mess. After a while, the door of the bedroom opened, but no minister came out to summon Wellington. Duchess Annorel walked out instead. She walked up to Wellington and stopped, with a sneer on her lips. Wellington said calmly, "I am honored to be received by the Duchess, but the one I want to see is His Majesty the Emperor." The Duchess said, "I am his advisor. His Majesty is not himself today." Wellington said, "You arrested General Nan Yi. If you execute him, then France will inevitably start another civil war. You have created a martyr of Nan Yi's name."

The Duchess could not help but stare with hatred and said, "I only seek revenge for my father and mother. You are trying to deprive the French monarch of the ability to avenge, so I hate you deeply. I will definitely get rid of you no matter what..." Wellington said, "If you execute General Nan Yi by firing squad, the future will be unthinkable." The Duchess said even more angrily, "That will be seen soon. He must be executed by firing squad!" Wellington restrained his anger and said coldly, "On the day that happens, I will expel you and the other advisors from the palace." The Duchess turned her head and said, "I will convey your words to His Majesty." She said and went in.

Inside the Royal Theatre of Paris, the lights were shining brightly, illuminating it as if it were daytime. Women in grand attire, the wives of Allied generals, accompanied by their majestic husbands, were seated in the boxes. In the special box in the middle, Duchess Annorel and the Duke of Cottoya, the brother of King Louis of France, were seated. Beside the royal box were the Prussian King and the Russian Tsar, etc. They were all surrounded by attendants and adjutants. In a smaller and less tea-splendorous box slightly away from Duchess Annorel, the Duke of Wellington and Duchess Francis were seated.

At this time, Wellington said to Francis, "I must say, it was a foolish thing for you to come to Paris. You have your husband; he is now in London." Francis looked at Wellington and said, "I came for you." Wellington said, "What difference does that make? You are still a little fool." At this moment, six pairs of eyes in the royal box were staring at the two of them. The owner of the third pair of eyes was a man with a rat's head and mouse eyes, and a shabby appearance. He was the Paris correspondent of a London newspaper. (To be continued)
